<em>b</em><sub>SIE</sub>, given <em>I</em><sub><em>i</em></sub>, <em>q</em>, and <em><img src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/icons/Entities/phgr.gif\" alt=\"phgr\" align=\"absmiddle\" /></em>\n</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table><p class=\"franklin fs-16\">\n\t\t\tDownload table as:\u00a0\n            <span class=\"btn-multi-block\"><a class=\"btn btn-primary wd-jnl-art-btn-ascii\" href=\"/0004-637X/803/2/71/suppdata/apj509959t1_ascii.txt?doi=10.1088/0004-637X/803/2/71\" target=\"_blank\">ASCII</a><a class=\"btn btn-primary wd-jnl-art-btn-typeset typeset-table-img\" href=\"/0004-637X/803/2/71/suppdata/apj509959t1_lr.gif\" target=\"_blank\">Typeset image</a></span></p></div><p>Following the same strategy used by Shu et al. (<a xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"cite\" href=\"#apj509959bib103\" id=\"fnref-apj509959bib103\">2012</a>), the likelihood function of hyperparameters,\u00a0<span xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"inline-eqn\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ieqn18.gif\" alt=\"${\\boldsymbol{ \\theta }} $\" align=\"top\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex\">{\\boldsymbol{ \\theta }}</script></span></span>, given the observed data,\u00a0<span xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"inline-eqn\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ieqn19.gif\" alt=\"$\\left\\{ d \\right\\}$\" align=\"top\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex\">\\left\\{ d \\right\\}</script></span></span>, and a hypothesis,\u00a0<span xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"inline-eqn\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ieqn20.gif\" alt=\"$\\mathcal{H}$\" align=\"top\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex\">\\mathcal{H}</script></span></span>, is defined as</p><div xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"display-eqn\" id=\"apj509959ueqn1\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ueqn1.gif\" alt=\"\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex; mode=display\">\\begin{eqnarray*}\\begin{array}{rcl} \\mathcal{L}\\left( {\\boldsymbol{ \\theta }} |\\left\\{ d \\right\\},\\mathcal{H} \\right) & \\equiv & {\\rm Pr} \\left( \\left\\{ d \\right\\}|{\\boldsymbol{ \\theta }} ,\\mathcal{H} \\right)=\\mathop{\\prod }\\limits_{i=0}^{N}\\;{\\rm Pr} \\left( {{y}_{i}},{{I}_{i}}|{\\boldsymbol{ \\theta }} ,\\mathcal{H} \\right) \\\\ {} & = & \\mathop{\\prod }\\limits_{i=0}^{N}\\iint {\\rm Pr} \\left( {{y}_{i}},{{I}_{i}}|y,x \\right){\\rm Pr} \\left( y,x|{\\boldsymbol{ \\theta }} ,\\mathcal{H} \\right)dxdy. \\\\ \\end{array}\\end{eqnarray*}</script></span></div><p>In general, <em>y</em> and <em>x</em> are independent variables, and <span xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"inline-eqn\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ieqn21.gif\" alt=\"${\\rm Pr} \\left( {{y}_{i}},{{x}_{i}}|y,x \\right)$\" align=\"top\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex\">{\\rm Pr} \\left( {{y}_{i}},{{x}_{i}}|y,x \\right)</script></span></span> can be split as</p><div xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"display-eqn\" id=\"apj509959eqn5\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959eqn5.gif\" alt=\"Equation (5)\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex; mode=display\">\\begin{eqnarray}\\begin{array}{rcl} \\mathcal{L}\\left( {\\boldsymbol{ \\theta }} |\\left\\{ d \\right\\},\\mathcal{H} \\right) & = & \\mathop{\\prod }\\limits_{i=0}^{N}\\iint {\\rm Pr} \\left( {{y}_{i}}|y \\right){\\rm Pr} \\left( {{I}_{i}}|x \\right){\\rm Pr} \\left( y,x|{\\boldsymbol{ \\theta }} ,\\mathcal{H} \\right)dxdy \\\\ {} & = & \\mathop{\\prod }\\limits_{i=0}^{N}\\iint {\\rm Pr} \\left( {{y}_{i}}|y \\right){\\rm Pr} \\left( y|x,a,b,\\delta ,\\mathcal{H} \\right){\\rm Pr} \\left( {{I}_{i}}|x \\right) \\\\ {} & {} & \\qquad {\\rm Pr} \\left( x \\right)dxdy. \\\\ \\end{array}\\end{eqnarray}\n\t\t\t\t\\tag{\n\t\t\t\t5\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t</script></span></div><p>The last two terms of the above equation are\u00a0related to the posterior PDF of <em>b</em><sub>SIE</sub> as</p><div xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"display-eqn\" id=\"apj509959eqn6\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959eqn6.gif\" alt=\"Equation (6)\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex; mode=display\">\\begin{eqnarray}&&{\\rm Pr} \\left( {{I}_{i}}|x \\right){\\rm Pr} \\left( x \\right)dx={\\rm Pr} \\left( {{b}_{{\\rm SIE}}}|{{I}_{i}} \\right){\\rm Pr} \\left( {{b}_{{\\rm SIE}}} \\right)d{{b}_{{\\rm SIE}}}.\\end{eqnarray}\n\t\t\t\t\\tag{\n\t\t\t\t6\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t</script></span></div><p>Then the likelihood function becomes</p><div xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"display-eqn\" id=\"apj509959eqn7\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959eqn7.gif\" alt=\"Equation (7)\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex; mode=display\">\\begin{eqnarray}&&\\begin{array}{l} \\mathcal{L}\\left( {\\boldsymbol{ \\theta }} |\\left\\{ d \\right\\},\\mathcal{H} \\right)=\\mathop{\\prod }\\limits_{i=0}^{N}\\iint \\iint dydqd{{\\phi }^{{}}}{\\rm d}{{{\\rm b}}_{{\\rm SIE}}}\\;{\\rm Pr} \\left( {{{\\rm y}}_{i}}|{\\rm y} \\right) \\\\ {\\rm Pr} \\left( y|x,a,b,\\delta ,\\mathcal{H} \\right){\\rm Pr} \\left( {{b}_{{\\rm SIE}}}|{{I}_{i}},q,\\phi \\right){{{\\rm Pr} }_{i}}\\left( q \\right){{{\\rm Pr} }_{i}}\\left( \\phi \\right). \\\\ \\end{array}\\end{eqnarray}\n\t\t\t\t\\tag{\n\t\t\t\t7\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t</script></span></div><p>\n</p><p>Looking at each term, <span xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"inline-eqn\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ieqn22.gif\" alt=\"${\\rm Pr} \\left( y|{{y}_{i}} \\right)$\" align=\"top\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex\">{\\rm Pr} \\left( y|{{y}_{i}} \\right)</script></span></span> is the likelihood function of <em>y</em> given <em>y</em><sub><em>i</em></sub>, which can be written as</p><div xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"display-eqn\" id=\"apj509959eqn8\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959eqn8.gif\" alt=\"Equation (8)\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex; mode=display\">\\begin{eqnarray}&&{\\rm Pr} \\left( {{y}_{i}}|y \\right)=\\frac{1}{\\sqrt{2\\pi }{{\\delta }_{i}}}{\\rm exp} \\left[ -\\frac{{{\\left( y-{{y}_{i}} \\right)}^{2}}}{2\\delta _{i}^{2}} \\right].\\end{eqnarray}\n\t\t\t\t\\tag{\n\t\t\t\t8\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t</script></span></div><p>\n<span xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"inline-eqn\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ieqn23.gif\" alt=\"${\\rm Pr} \\left( y|x,a,b,\\delta ,\\mathcal{H} \\right)$\" align=\"top\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex\">{\\rm Pr} \\left( y|x,a,b,\\delta ,\\mathcal{H} \\right)</script></span></span> is the conditional PDF of <em>y</em> given <em>x</em> and three hyperparameters. Following the parameterized model stated by Equation (<a xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"eqnref\" href=\"#apj509959eqn4\">4</a>), <span xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"inline-eqn\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ieqn24.gif\" alt=\"${\\rm Pr} \\left( y|x,a,b,\\delta ,\\mathcal{H} \\right)$\" align=\"top\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex\">{\\rm Pr} \\left( y|x,a,b,\\delta ,\\mathcal{H} \\right)</script></span></span> can be expressed as</p><div xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"display-eqn\" id=\"apj509959eqn9\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959eqn9.gif\" alt=\"Equation (9)\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex; mode=display\">\\begin{eqnarray}&&\\begin{array}{l} {\\rm Pr} \\left( y|x,a,b,\\delta ,\\mathcal{H} \\right)=\\frac{1}{\\sqrt{2\\pi }\\delta } \\\\ \\quad \\times {\\rm exp} \\left\\{ -\\frac{{{\\left[ a\\left( x-2.35 \\right)+b-\\left( y-2.35 \\right) \\right]}^{2}}}{2{{\\delta }^{2}}} \\right\\}, \\\\ \\end{array}\\end{eqnarray}\n\t\t\t\t\\tag{\n\t\t\t\t9\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t</script></span></div><p>with an assumed intrinsic scatter,\u00a0<em>\u03b4,</em> in <em>y</em>. <span xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"inline-eqn\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ieqn25.gif\" alt=\"${\\rm Pr} \\left( y|x,a,b,\\delta ,\\mathcal{H} \\right)$\" align=\"top\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex\">{\\rm Pr} \\left( y|x,a,b,\\delta ,\\mathcal{H} \\right)</script></span></span> is of physical interest, as it quantifies the relation between <em>y</em> and <em>x</em> and can be adopted in related studies. <span xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"inline-eqn\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ieqn26.gif\" alt=\"${\\rm Pr} \\left( {{b}_{{\\rm SIE}}}|{{I}_{i}},q,\\phi \\right)$\" align=\"top\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex\">{\\rm Pr} \\left( {{b}_{{\\rm SIE}}}|{{I}_{i}},q,\\phi \\right)</script></span></span> is the posterior PDF of <em>b</em><sub>SIE</sub>, as returned by <span class=\"small-caps\">MultiNest,</span> given the imaging data,\u00a0<em>I</em><sub><em>i</em></sub>, axis ratio,\u00a0<em>q</em>, and position angle,\u00a0<em><img src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/icons/Entities/phgr.gif\" alt=\"phgr\" align=\"absmiddle\" /></em>. Pr<sub><em>i</em></sub> (<em>q</em>) and Pr<sub><em>i</em></sub> (<em><img src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/icons/Entities/phgr.gif\" alt=\"phgr\" align=\"absmiddle\" /></em>) are the prior PDFs of <em>q</em> and <em><img src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/icons/Entities/phgr.gif\" alt=\"phgr\" align=\"absmiddle\" /></em> for the <em>i</em>th lens galaxy, which are assumed to be uniform distributions.</p><p>The integration over <em>y</em> can be easily done and yields</p><div xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"display-eqn\" id=\"apj509959eqn10\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959eqn10.gif\" alt=\"Equation (10)\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex; mode=display\">\\begin{eqnarray}&&\\begin{array}{l} \\mathcal{L}=\\mathop{\\prod }\\limits_{i=0}^{N}\\iiint dqd{{\\phi }^{{}}}d{{b}_{{\\rm SIE}}}\\;\\frac{{\\rm exp} \\left[ -{{\\left( {\\rm \\ \\Delta\\ }-{{y}_{i}} \\right)}^{2}}/\\left( 2\\left( \\sigma _{i}^{2}+{{\\delta }^{2}} \\right) \\right) \\right]}{\\sqrt{2\\pi \\left( \\sigma _{i}^{2}+{{\\delta }^{2}} \\right)}} \\\\ \\qquad \\quad {\\rm Pr} \\left( {{b}_{{\\rm SIE}}}|{{I}_{i}},q,\\phi \\right){{{\\rm Pr} }_{i}}\\left( q \\right){{{\\rm Pr} }_{i}}\\left( \\phi \\right), \\\\ \\end{array}\\end{eqnarray}\n\t\t\t\t\\tag{\n\t\t\t\t10\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t</script></span></div><p>where \u0394 = <em>a</em> <b>&#x00d7;</b> [<em>x</em>(<em>b</em><sub>SIE</sub>) \u2212 2.35] + <em>b</em> + 2.35.</p><p>For grade-A lenses, we can treat <span xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"inline-eqn\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ieqn27.gif\" alt=\"${\\rm Pr} \\left( {{b}_{{\\rm SIE}}}|{{I}_{i}},q,\\phi \\right)$\" align=\"top\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex\">{\\rm Pr} \\left( {{b}_{{\\rm SIE}}}|{{I}_{i}},q,\\phi \\right)</script></span></span>, Pr<sub><em>i</em></sub>(<em>q</em>), and Pr<sub><em>i</em></sub>(<em><img src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/icons/Entities/phgr.gif\" alt=\"phgr\" align=\"absmiddle\" /></em>) as delta functions. The likelihood contribution from grade-A lenses is</p><div xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"display-eqn\" id=\"apj509959eqn11\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959eqn11.gif\" alt=\"Equation (11)\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex; mode=display\">\\begin{eqnarray}\\begin{array}{rcl} {\\rm ln} {{\\mathcal{L}}_{A}} & = & -\\mathop{\\sum }\\limits_{i=0}^{{{N}_{A}}}\\{\\frac{{{\\left( {\\rm \\ \\Delta\\ }\\left( b_{{\\rm SIE}}^{i} \\right)-{{y}_{i}} \\right)}^{2}}}{2\\left( \\sigma _{i}^{2}+{{\\delta }^{2}} \\right)}+0.5 \\\\ {} & {} & \\times {\\rm ln} \\left[ 2\\pi \\left( \\sigma _{i}^{2}+{{\\delta }^{2}} \\right) \\right]\\}. \\\\ \\end{array}\\end{eqnarray}\n\t\t\t\t\\tag{\n\t\t\t\t11\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t</script></span></div><p>For the <em>i</em>th grade-C lens, <span class=\"small-caps\">MultiNest</span> generates samples of <span xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"inline-eqn\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ieqn28.gif\" alt=\"$b_{{\\rm SIE}}^{ij}$\" align=\"top\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex\">b_{{\\rm SIE}}^{ij}</script></span></span> with derived posteriors (or weights),\u00a0<span xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"inline-eqn\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ieqn29.gif\" alt=\"${\\rm Pr} \\left( b_{{\\rm SIE}}^{ij}|{{I}_{i}},q,\\phi \\right)$\" align=\"top\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex\">{\\rm Pr} \\left( b_{{\\rm SIE}}^{ij}|{{I}_{i}},q,\\phi \\right)</script></span></span>. The likelihood contribution is therefore approximated as</p><div xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"display-eqn\" id=\"apj509959eqn12\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959eqn12.gif\" alt=\"Equation (12)\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex; mode=display\">\\begin{eqnarray}\\begin{array}{rcl} {\\rm ln} {{\\mathcal{L}}_{C}} & = & \\mathop{\\sum }\\limits_{i=0}^{{{N}_{C}}}{\\rm ln} \\\\ {} & {} & \\{\\mathop{\\sum }\\limits_{j=0}^{N}\\frac{{\\rm exp} \\left[ -{{\\left( {\\rm \\ \\Delta\\ }\\left( b_{{\\rm SIE}}^{ij} \\right)-{{y}_{i}} \\right)}^{2}}/\\left( 2\\left( \\sigma _{i}^{2}+{{\\delta }^{2}} \\right) \\right) \\right]}{\\sqrt{2\\pi \\left( \\sigma _{i}^{2}+{{\\delta }^{2}} \\right)}} \\\\ {} & {} & \\times {\\rm Pr} \\left( b_{{\\rm SIE}}^{ij}|{{I}_{i}},q,\\phi \\right)\\}. \\\\ \\end{array}\\end{eqnarray}\n\t\t\t\t\\tag{\n\t\t\t\t12\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t</script></span></div><p>The posterior PDF of the hyperparameters that we are interested in is simply related to the likelihood via the <em>Bayes' rule</em> as</p><div xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"display-eqn\" id=\"apj509959eqn13\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959eqn13.gif\" alt=\"Equation (13)\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex; mode=display\">\\begin{eqnarray}\\begin{array}{ccccccccccccccc} {\\rm Pr} \\left( {\\boldsymbol{ \\theta }} |\\left\\{ d \\right\\},\\mathcal{H} \\right) & = & \\frac{{\\rm Pr} \\left( \\left\\{ d \\right\\}|{\\boldsymbol{ \\theta }} ,\\mathcal{H} \\right)\\;{\\rm Pr} \\left( {\\boldsymbol{ \\theta }} |\\mathcal{H} \\right)}{{\\rm Pr} \\left( \\left\\{ d \\right\\}|\\mathcal{H} \\right)} \\\\ {} & = & \\frac{\\mathcal{L}\\left( {\\boldsymbol{ \\theta }} |\\left\\{ d \\right\\},\\mathcal{H} \\right)\\;{\\rm Pr} \\left( {\\boldsymbol{ \\theta }} |\\mathcal{H} \\right)}{{\\rm Pr} \\left( \\left\\{ d \\right\\}|\\mathcal{H} \\right)}, \\\\ \\end{array}\\quad \\end{eqnarray}\n\t\t\t\t\\tag{\n\t\t\t\t13\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t</script></span></div><p>from which we can infer the relation between <span xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"inline-eqn\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ieqn30.gif\" alt=\"${{{\\rm log} }_{10}}{{\\sigma }_{*}}$\" align=\"top\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex\">{{{\\rm log} }_{10}}{{\\sigma }_{*}}</script></span></span> and <span xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"inline-eqn\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959ieqn31.gif\" alt=\"${{{\\rm log} }_{10}}{{\\sigma }_{{\\rm SIE}}}$\" align=\"top\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex\">{{{\\rm log} }_{10}}{{\\sigma }_{{\\rm SIE}}}</script></span></span>.</p><p>Known as <em>f</em><sub>SIE</sub>, the ratio of <em>\u03c3</em><sub>*</sub> to <em>\u03c3</em><sub>SIE</sub> has been used as an empirical estimator of the logarithmic mass\u2013density slope,\u00a0<em>\u03b3</em>' (Treu et al. <a xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"cite\" href=\"#apj509959bib117\" id=\"fnref-apj509959bib117\">2009</a>; Auger et al. <a xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"cite\" href=\"#apj509959bib6\" id=\"fnref-apj509959bib6\">2010a</a>). Using the <em>\u03c3</em><sub>*</sub>\u2013<em>\u03c3</em><sub>SIE</sub> relation found above, by definition, we have</p><div xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"display-eqn\" id=\"apj509959eqn14\"><span class=\"tex\"><span class=\"texImage\"><img src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959eqn14.gif\" alt=\"Equation (14)\"></img></span><script type=\"math/tex; mode=display\">\\begin{eqnarray}\\begin{array}{rcl} {{f}_{{\\rm SIE}}}=\\frac{{{\\sigma }_{*}}}{{{\\sigma }_{{\\rm SIE}}}}={{10}^{y-x}} & = & {{10}^{\\left[ \\left( a-1 \\right)\\left( y-2.35 \\right)+b \\right]/a}} \\\\ {} & = & {{10}^{\\left( a-1 \\right)\\left( x-2.35 \\right)+b}}. \\\\ \\end{array}\\end{eqnarray}\n\t\t\t\t\\tag{\n\t\t\t\t14\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t</script></span></div><p>The physical interpretation of hyperparameters <em>a</em> and <em>b</em> then become straightforward. If <em>a</em> is exactly unity, <em>f</em><sub>SIE</sub> (or equivalently the logarithmic mass\u2013density slope <em>\u03b3</em>') is independent of <em>\u03c3</em><sub>*</sub>, an indicator of the mass of lens galaxies. A less-than-unity <em>a</em> indicates an anticorrelation between <em>\u03b3</em>' and <em>\u03c3</em>*, namely, galaxies with smaller/larger <em>\u03c3</em>* are more/less centrally concentrated. <em>b</em> is related to the <em>f</em><sub>SIE</sub> value at the mean <em>\u03c3</em><sub>SIE</sub> value (<em>\u03c3</em><sub>SIE</sub> \u2248 220 km s<sup>\u22121</sup>). The mass\u2013density profile is (approximately speaking) isothermal if <em>b</em>  =  0, subisothermal if <em>b</em> &lt; 0, and superisothermal if <em>b</em> &gt; 0. </p><p>Marginalizing over the <em>\u03b4</em> dimension, the 2D posterior PDF of <em>a</em> and <em>b</em> is shown in Figure <a xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" href=\"#apj509959f6\">6</a>. There are three sets of contours for the grade-A subsample (dashed gray), grade-C subsample (dotted gray), and the combined sample (solid black). The marginal PDFs of <em>a</em> and <em>b</em> are obtained by marginalizing over either <em>b</em> or <em>a</em> and shown in Figure <a xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" href=\"#apj509959f7\">7</a>. The best-estimated values for <em>a</em> and <em>b</em> and the uncertainties are extracted from simple Gaussian fits to the corresponding marginal PDFs\u00a0and summarized in Table <a xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" class=\"tabref\" href=\"#apj509959t2\">2</a>.</p><figure xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" id=\"apj509959f6\" tabindex=\"-1\" role=\"group\" class=\"boxout boxout-bdr-grey keyboard-focus-only\" data-toolbar-type=\"figure\" data-toolbar-link=\"apj509959f6\" data-toolbar-img=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959f6_lr.jpg\" data-toolbar-title=\"Figure 6.\"><figure><div class=\"panzoom-container\"><div class=\"panzoom-parent\" style=\"overflow: hidden; position: relative;\"><img class=\"panzoom\" alt=\"Figure 6.\" src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959f6_lr.jpg\" style=\"transform: matrix(1, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0); backface-visibility: hidden; transform-origin: 50% 50% 0px; cursor: move; transition: transform 200ms ease-in-out 0s;\"></img></div><div class=\"buttons zoom-tools\"><button class=\"zoom-in\"><span class=\"icon-zoomin\"></span>\n\t                 Zoom In\n\t\t\t\t</button><button class=\"zoom-out\"><span class=\"icon-zoomout\"></span>\n\t                 Zoom Out\n\t\t\t\t</button><span class=\"mobile-block\"><button class=\"reset\"><span class=\"icon-loop\"></span>\n\t                     Reset image size\n\t\t\t\t\t</button></span></div></div><figcaption><div class=\"article-text figure-caption\"><p><strong>Figure 6.</strong>\u00a0Posterior PDFs for\u00a0(<em>a</em>, <em>b</em>) the combined sample (solid black contours), grade-A subsample (dashed gray contours), and grade-C subsample (dotted gray contours). The 68, 95, and 99.7% confidence levels are plotted accordingly. The horizontal line (<em>b</em> = \u22120.0338, as suggested by the empirical relation in Auger et al. (<a class=\"cite\" href=\"#apj509959bib6\" id=\"fnref-apj509959bib6\">2010a</a>)) corresponds to an isothermal mass\u2013density profile at <em>\u03c3</em><sub>SIE</sub> \u2248 220 km s<sup>\u22121</sup>, and the vertical line (<em>a</em> = 1) corresponds to a velocity-dispersion-independent mass\u2013density profile.</p></div><p class=\"mb-05 print-hide\">Download figure:</p><span class=\"btn-multi-block print-hide\"><a class=\"btn btn-primary fig-dwnld-std-img\" id=\"wd-jnl-art-btn-std-img-apj509959f6\" href=\"/0004-637X/803/2/71/downloadFigure/figure/apj509959f6\"><span class=\"icon-image\"></span> Standard image\n\t\t\t\t\t</a><a class=\"btn btn-primary fig-dwnld-hi-img\" id=\"wd-jnl-art-btn-hires-img-apj509959f6\" href=\"/0004-637X/803/2/71/downloadHRFigure/figure/apj509959f6\"><span class=\"icon-image\"></span> High-resolution image\n\t\t\t\t\t</a></span></figcaption></figure></figure><figure xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" id=\"apj509959f7\" tabindex=\"-1\" role=\"group\" class=\"boxout boxout-bdr-grey keyboard-focus-only\" data-toolbar-type=\"figure\" data-toolbar-link=\"apj509959f7\" data-toolbar-img=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959f7_lr.jpg\" data-toolbar-title=\"Figure 7.\"><figure><div class=\"panzoom-container\"><div class=\"panzoom-parent\" style=\"overflow: hidden; position: relative;\"><img class=\"panzoom\" alt=\"Figure 7.\" src=\"https://static.iopscience.com/2.44.0/img/lazy-loading-placeholder.gif\" data-src=\"https://cdn.iopscience.com/images/0004-637X/803/2/71/Full/apj509959f7_lr.jpg\" style=\"transform: matrix(1, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0); backface-visibility: hidden; transform-origin: 50% 50% 0px; cursor: move; transition: transform 200ms ease-in-out 0s;\"></img></div><div class=\"buttons zoom-tools\"><button class=\"zoom-in\"><span class=\"icon-zoomin\"></span>\n\t                 Zoom In\n\t\t\t\t</button><button class=\"zoom-out\"><span class=\"icon-zoomout\"></span>\n\t                 Zoom Out\n\t\t\t\t</button><span class=\"mobile-block\"><button class=\"reset\"><span class=\"icon-loop\"></span>\n\t                     Reset image size\n\t\t\t\t\t</button></span></div></div><figcaption><div class=\"article-text figure-caption\"><p><strong>Figure 7.</strong>\u00a0Marginal PDFs of <em>a</em> and <em>b</em> for the combined sample (grade-A+C lenses, solid black curves) and grade-A lens subsample (dashed gray curves). Dotted lines correspond\u00a0to the peak positions in the marginal PDFs.</p></div><p class=\"mb-05 print-hide\">Download figure:</p><span class=\"btn-multi-block print-hide\"><a class=\"btn class=\"icon-image\"></span> High-resolution image\n\t\t\t\t\t</a></span></figcaption></figure></figure><div tabindex=\"-1\" id=\"apj509959t2\" class=\"boxout boxout-bdr-grey keyboard-focus-only\"><p><b>Table 2.</b>\u00a0\nBest-estimated Values of the Hyperparameters <em>a</em> and <em>b</em>\n\n</p><table cellpadding=\"0\" cellspacing=\"0\" border=\"0\" data-toolbar-link=\"apj509959t2\" data-toolbar-img=\"/0004-637X/803/2/71/suppdata/apj509959t2_lr.gif\" data-toolbar-type=\"table\" data-toolbar-title=\"Table 2\"><colgroup><col align=\"left\"
